 (also from input agencies) jise zyaadaatar log nuksaan kii vajah maanate hai, usee baat ko chunavi ranneetikaar prashanth kishor ek avasar maan rahe hai
 
 
 Yes, we are talking about Sheila Dixit, 78, who has been declared the Chief Ministerial candidate for the Uttar Pradesh by the Congress
 
 
 prashanth kishor ke kareebi sutron kaa kahana he ki dilli kii teen kaarykaal tak mukhyamantri raheen shila dikshit kii umr ko uttar pradesh main 'tajurbe ke pratik' or 'bhaavnaatmak apil' ke rup main istemaal karne ke liye ek khaas naaraa banaaya gaya he - "mere jivan kaa ek hi sapana, uttar pradesh ko dilli jaisaa bananaa
 
 
 " shila ke naam kii aupchaarik ghoshnaa congress ne guuruuvaar ko hi kii he, lekin usase kai hafte pehle se ek taraf se mil rahe sanketon or duusari ore se mil rahe khandanon ne ghoshnaa ke utsaah ko kaaphi kam kar diya, or is baat ko shila khud bhi kabool karti hai
 Speaking to NDTV, he said, "it would have been great if it (the decision to make the chief ministerial candidate) had been decided earlier
" 
 
 lekin chunki aisa nahin hua he, to hamen ab jo bhi vakt bachaa he, uskaa behtareen istemaal karnaa hoga
 
 
 " sutron kaa kahana he ki shila dikshit kii tulana main aadhi se bhi kam umr ke 37-varshiya prashanth kishor uttar pradesh vidhansabha chunaav ke dauraan dilli kii mukhyamantri ke rup main shila ke teen kaarykalon ke bare main jorshor se prachaar karenge
 
 
 By the way, in addition to his achievements as a politician, Prashant will also draw the attention of the people of UP to the fact that Sheila Dixit is married in a Brahmin family, so as to assimilate upper caste votes towards Congress
 prashanth kishor ko chunavi ranneeti visheshgy ke rup main varsh 2014 ke loksabhaa chunaav ne sthapit kiya tha, jisamen unhone pradhanmantri narendra modi ke liye ranneeti taiyaar kii thi, jisaki madad se bhartiya janata party (bijepi) ne shandaar jeet hasil kii thi
 Prashant then parted ways with the BJP and joined hands with Bihar Chief Minister Nitish Kumar for the assembly elections held last year, and became the chief minister for a third consecutive term as CM
 iske baad prashanth ab punjab or uttar pradesh ke vidhansabha chunaavon ke liye congress kii ranneeti bana rahe hai
 There were also reports that Prashant Kishore is struggling against indecision and heiraki (hierarchy) present in the Congress, but Prashant's close people have denied that he would be with the film actor as state unit president Raj Babbar, who turned politician, was against being elected
 film abhinayta ke rup main kaamyaab pari khilne ke baad raaj babbar samaajawaadee party ke netaa bane the, or phir varsh 2008 main congress se jude or kuch hi maheene baad unhone apni mahatta sabit kar di, jab unhone samaajawaadee party pramukh mulaayam singh yadav kii putravadhu or mukhyamantri akhilesh yadav kii patni dimpal yadav ko haraakar ek loksabhaa seat jeet lee
 So now, where Raj Babbar's star appeal will be redeemed across the state
 vahiin prashanth kishor ke kareebi sutron kaa kahana he ki congress prachaar samiti ke pramukh banaae gaye sanjay singh amethi or aasapaas ke ilaakon main party kaaryakartaaon main utsaah kaa sanchaar karne main safal rahenge
 Sanjay is part of Amethi's former royal family, and Amethi Lok Sabha seat is the constituency of Rahul Gandhi, who is accountable only to his mother and party president Sonia Gandhi as the number two in the party, that is, vice-president
 yahaan ek baat yah bhi dhyaan dene laayak he ki sanjay singh ko darkinar kiya janaa nuksaandaayak bhi ho saktaa tha, kyonki vah ek baar congress ko chhodkar bijepi main shaamil ho chuke hai, or varsh 2003 main congress main laute the
 After this, he was made a Rajya Sabha member in the year 2014, because it seemed that he was preparing to leave the party again
 tippaniyan Apart from Uttar Pradesh, Prashant Kishore is also preparing the party's strategy for the Punjab assembly elections, where the image of the ruling bjp-akali Dal government has not been very good
 lekin philhal dilli ke maujuuda mukhyamantri arvind kejariwal or unki aam aadmi party punjab main logon kaa dhyaan khinchne main zyaada kaamyaab rahi he
 The Aam Aadmi Party won four Lok Sabha seats from Punjab, despite being just two years old during the 2014 Lok Sabha elections
 vaise, yahaan bhi prashanth kishor ko ek varisht umrdaraj netaa kaa hi prachaar karnaa pad rahaa he
 Prashant Kishore has also chanted for the promotion of 74-year-old Captain Amarinder Singh, who is considered as the Chief Ministerial candidate from the Congress - "I have only one dream, make Punjab strong
" 
 
 " Sources close to Prashant Kishore say that a special slogan has been coined to use the age of Sheila Dixit, who was Chief Minister of Delhi for three terms, as a 'symbol of experience' and 'emotional appeal' in Uttar Pradesh - "my One dream of life, making Uttar Pradesh like Delhi
 
 
 " Sheila's name has been formally announced by the Congress on Thursday, but several weeks before that, the signs from one side and the rebuttals from the other side has greatly reduced the enthusiasm of the declaration, and this she herself too She confesses
 NDTV se baatcheet main unhone kaha, "badhiya hota, agar yah (mukhyamantri pad kii ummidavaar banane kaa faisla) pehle tay kar liya gaya hota
 
 
 But since this has not happened, then we have to make best use of whatever time is left
 
 
 " Sources say that 37-year-old Prashant Kishore, less than half the age of Sheila Dixit, will campaign vigorously about Sheila's three terms as Chief Minister of Delhi during the Uttar Pradesh Assembly elections
 
 
 vaise, rajaneta ke rup main unki uplabdhiyon ke atirikt prashanth is ore bhi upi kii janata kaa dhyaan aakarshith karenge ki shila dikshit kaa vivaah brahman parivaar main hua he, taaki oonchi jati ke voton ko congress kii ore sameta ja sake
 Prashant Kishore was established as an election strategy expert by the 2014 Lok Sabha elections, in which he devised a strategy for Prime Minister Narendra Modi, with the help of which the Bharatiya Janata Party (BJP) won a landslide victory
 iske baad prashanth ne bijepi se naata todakar pichley saal hue vidhansabha chunaav ke liye bihar ke mukhyamantri nitish kumaar se haath milaayaa tha, or siem ke rup main unhen lagaataar teesraa kaarykaal dilaane ke nimitt bane
 After this, Prashant is now preparing the Congress strategy for the assembly elections in Punjab and Uttar Pradesh
 is tarah kii khabaren bhi aa rahi thim ki prashanth kishor ko congress main maujuud anirnay or herarki (padanukram) ke khilaaf jujhna pad rahaa he, lekin prashanth ke karibiyon ne is baat kaa khandan kiya he ki vah pradesh ikai adhyaksh ke rup main film abhinayta se rajaneta bane raaj babbar ko chune jane ke khilaaf the
 Raj Babbar became a leader of the Samajwadi Party after playing a successful innings as a film actor, and then joined the Congress in 2008 and a few months later proved his worth when he was the daughter-in-law of Samajwadi Party chief Mulayam Singh Yadav and Won one Lok Sabha seat by defeating Dimple Yadav, wife of Chief Minister Akhilesh Yadav
 so, ab jahaan ek ore raaj babbar kii star apil rajyabar main bhunaai jaaegi
 On the other hand, sources close to Prashant Kishore say that Sanjay Singh, who was made the head of the Congress campaign committee, will be able to communicate enthusiasm among the party workers in Amethi and surrounding areas
 sanjay amethi ke purv rajpariwaar kaa hissaa hai, or amethi loksabhaa seat rahul gandhi kaa chunaav kshetra he, jo party main number do, yani upaadhyaksh kii haisiyat se sirf apni maa or party adhyaksh sonia gandhi ko javabdeh hai
 It is also worth noting that bypassing Sanjay Singh could have been detrimental as he has once left the Congress and joined the BJP, and returned to the Congress in the year 2003
 iske baad unhen varsh 2014 main rajyasabha sadsy banwaaya gaya tha, kyonki lagane laga tha ki vah phir party ko chhodkar jane kii taiyaari kar rahe hai
 The comments uttar pradesh ke alaava prashanth kishor punjab vidhansabha chunaav ke liye bhi party kii ranneeti taiyaar kar rahe hai, jahaan sattashin bijepi-akali dal sarkaar kii chhavi kuch khaas acchhee nahin rahi he
 But currently Delhi's current Chief Minister Arvind Kejriwal and his Aam Aadmi Party have been more successful in grabbing the attention of the people in Punjab
 varsh 2014 ke loksabhaa chunaav ke dauraan sirf do saal puraani party hone ke baavjood aam aadmi party ne punjab se chaar loksabhaa siten jiti thim
 By the way, here too, Prashant Kishore has to promote only a senior aged leader
 congress kii ore se mukhyamantri pad ke daavedaar maane ja rahe 74-varshiya captain amarinder singh ke prachaar ke liye bhi prashanth kishor ne naaraa banaaya he - "meraa ek hi sapana he, punjab ko majboot bananaa
